Grate the zucchini , sprinkle it with salt and toss well . Place in a colander to drain for 30 minutes . Over a bowl , squeeze the zucchini and save liquid . Preheat oven to 350 . In a large skillet melt the butter over medium heat . Add the onion , garlic and zucchini and cook for 10 minutes . Add the flour and tarragon and cook over medium low heat for 5 more minutes . Stir in the reserved zucchini liquid and cook until thickened	Cool to lukewarm	Yes

Place in a greased bowl , tuning once to grease top . Cover and let rise in a warm place until doubled , about 1 14 / hours / . Punch down . Shape into a loaf	Place into a greased 9x5x3-inch loaf pan	Yes

Reduce the heat to medium-low	Broil for 3 to 5 minutes or until golden brown and set	No
